<p><strong>83:14</strong> — كَلَّا‌ۖ بَلۡۜ رَانَ عَلَىٰ قُلُوبِهِم مَّا كَانُو<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>اۡ</span> يَكۡسِبُونَ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>83:16</strong> — ثُمَّ إِنَّهُمۡ لَصَالُو<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>اۡ</span> ٱلۡجَحِيمِ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>83:29</strong> — إِنَّ ٱلَّذِينَ أَجۡرَمُو<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>اۡ</span> كَانُو<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>اۡ</span> مِنَ ٱلَّذِينَ ءَامَنُو<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>اۡ</span> يَضۡحَكُونَ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 3)</span></p>
<p><strong>83:30</strong> — وَإِذَا مَرُّو<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>اۡ</span> بِهِمۡ يَتَغَامَزُونَ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>83:31</strong> — وَإِذَا ٱنقَلَبُوٓ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>اۡ</span> إِلَىٰٓ أَهۡلِهِمُ ٱنقَلَبُو<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>اۡ</span> فَكِهِينَ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 2)</span></p>
<p><strong>83:32</strong> — وَإِذَا رَأَوۡهُمۡ قَالُوٓ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>اۡ</span> إِنَّ هَـٰٓؤُلَآءِ لَضَآلُّونَ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>83:33</strong> — وَمَآ أُرۡسِلُو<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>اۡ</span> عَلَيۡهِمۡ حَـٰفِظِينَ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>83:34</strong> — فَٱلۡيَوۡمَ ٱلَّذِينَ ءَامَنُو<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>اۡ</span> مِنَ ٱلۡكُفَّارِ يَضۡحَكُونَ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>83:36</strong> — هَلۡ ثُوِّبَ ٱلۡكُفَّارُ مَا كَانُو<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>اۡ</span> يَفۡعَلُونَ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>84:11</strong> — فَسَوۡفَ يَدۡعُو<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>اۡ</span> ثُبُورًا <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>84:22</strong> — بَلِ ٱلَّذِينَ كَفَرُو<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>اۡ</span> يُكَذِّبُونَ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>84:25</strong> — إِلَّا ٱلَّذِينَ ءَامَنُو<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>اۡ</span> وَعَمِلُو<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>اۡ</span> ٱلصَّـٰلِحَـٰتِ لَهُمۡ أَجۡرٌ غَيۡرُ مَمۡنُونِۭ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 2)</span></p>
<p><strong>85:8</strong> — وَمَا نَقَمُو<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>اۡ</span> مِنۡهُمۡ إِلَّآ أَن يُؤۡمِنُو<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>اۡ</span> بِٱللَّهِ ٱلۡعَزِيزِ ٱلۡحَمِيدِ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 2)</span></p>
<p><strong>85:10</strong> — إِنَّ ٱلَّذِينَ فَتَنُو<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>اۡ</span> ٱلۡمُؤۡمِنِينَ وَٱلۡمُؤۡمِنَـٰتِ ثُمَّ لَمۡ يَتُوبُو<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>اۡ</span> فَلَهُمۡ عَذَابُ جَهَنَّمَ وَلَهُمۡ عَذَابُ ٱلۡحَرِيقِ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 2)</span></p>
<p><strong>85:11</strong> — إِنَّ ٱلَّذِينَ ءَامَنُو<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>اۡ</span> وَعَمِلُو<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>اۡ</span> ٱلصَّـٰلِحَـٰتِ لَهُمۡ جَنَّـٰتٌ تَجۡرِى مِن تَحۡتِهَا ٱلۡأَنۡهَـٰرُ‌ۚ ذ<rule class=custom_alef_maksora>ٰ</rule>لِكَ ٱلۡفَوۡزُ ٱلۡكَبِيرُ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 2)</span></p>
<p><strong>85:19</strong> — بَلِ ٱلَّذِينَ كَفَرُو<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>اۡ</span> فِى تَكۡذِيبٍ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>87:16</strong> — بَلۡ تُؤۡثِرُونَ ٱلۡحَيَ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>و</span>ٰةَ ٱلدُّنۡيَا <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>89:9</strong> — وَثَمُودَ ٱلَّذِينَ جَابُو<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>اۡ</span> ٱلصَّخۡرَ بِٱلۡوَادِ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>89:11</strong> — ٱلَّذِينَ طَغَوۡ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>اۡ</span> فِى ٱلۡبِلَـٰدِ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>89:12</strong> — فَأَكۡثَرُو<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>اۡ</span> فِيهَا ٱلۡفَسَادَ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>89:23</strong> — وَجِ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>اۡ</span>ىٓءَ يَوۡمَئِذِۭ بِجَهَنَّمَ‌ۚ يَوۡمَئِذٍ يَتَذَكَّرُ ٱلۡإِنسَـٰنُ وَأَنَّىٰ لَهُ ٱلذِّكۡرَىٰ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>90:17</strong> — ثُمَّ كَانَ مِنَ ٱلَّذِينَ ءَامَنُو<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>اۡ</span> وَتَوَاصَوۡ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>اۡ</span> بِٱلصَّبۡرِ وَتَوَاصَوۡ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>اۡ</span> بِٱلۡمَرۡحَمَةِ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 3)</span></p>
<p><strong>90:18</strong> — أُ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>وۡ</span>لَـٰٓئِكَ أَصۡحَـٰبُ ٱلۡمَيۡمَنَةِ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>90:19</strong> — وَٱلَّذِينَ كَفَرُو<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>اۡ</span> بِـَٔـايَـٰتِنَا هُمۡ أَصۡحَـٰبُ ٱلۡمَشۡــَٔمَةِ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>95:6</strong> — إِلَّا ٱلَّذِينَ ءَامَنُو<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>اۡ</span> وَعَمِلُو<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>اۡ</span> ٱلصَّـٰلِحَـٰتِ فَلَهُمۡ أَجۡرٌ غَيۡرُ مَمۡنُونٍ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 2)</span></p>
<p><strong>98:1</strong> — لَمۡ يَكُنِ ٱلَّذِينَ كَفَرُو<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>اۡ</span> مِنۡ أَهۡلِ ٱلۡكِتَـٰبِ وَٱلۡمُشۡرِكِينَ مُنفَكِّينَ حَتَّىٰ تَأۡتِيَهُمُ ٱلۡبَيِّنَةُ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>98:2</strong> — رَسُولٌ مِّنَ ٱللَّهِ يَتۡلُو<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>اۡ</span> صُحُفًا مُّطَهَّرَةً <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>98:4</strong> — وَمَا تَفَرَّقَ ٱلَّذِينَ أُوتُو<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>اۡ</span> ٱلۡكِتَـٰبَ إِلَّا مِنۢ بَعۡدِ مَا جَآءَتۡهُمُ ٱلۡبَيِّنَةُ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>98:5</strong> — وَمَآ أُمِرُوٓ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>اۡ</span> إِلَّا لِيَعۡبُدُو<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>اۡ</span> ٱللَّهَ مُخۡلِصِينَ لَهُ ٱلدِّينَ حُنَفَآءَ وَيُقِيمُو<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>اۡ</span> ٱلصَّلَ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>و</span>ٰةَ وَيُؤۡتُو<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>اۡ</span> ٱلزَّكَ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>و</span>ٰةَ‌ۚ وَذ<rule class=custom_alef_maksora>ٰ</rule>لِكَ دِينُ ٱلۡقَيِّمَةِ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 6)</span></p>
<p><strong>98:6</strong> — إِنَّ ٱلَّذِينَ كَفَرُو<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>اۡ</span> مِنۡ أَهۡلِ ٱلۡكِتَـٰبِ وَٱلۡمُشۡرِكِينَ فِى نَارِ جَهَنَّمَ خَـٰلِدِينَ فِيهَآ‌ۚ أُ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>وۡ</span>لَـٰٓئِكَ هُمۡ شَرُّ ٱلۡبَرِيَّةِ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 2)</span></p>
<p><strong>98:7</strong> — إِنَّ ٱلَّذِينَ ءَامَنُو<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>اۡ</span> وَعَمِلُو<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>اۡ</span> ٱلصَّـٰلِحَـٰتِ أُ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>وۡ</span>لَـٰٓئِكَ هُمۡ خَيۡرُ ٱلۡبَرِيَّةِ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 3)</span></p>
<p><strong>98:8</strong> — جَزَآؤُهُمۡ عِندَ رَبِّهِمۡ جَنَّـٰتُ عَدۡنٍ تَجۡرِى مِن تَحۡتِهَا ٱلۡأَنۡهَـٰرُ خَـٰلِدِينَ فِيهَآ أَبَدًا‌ۖ رَّضِىَ ٱللَّهُ عَنۡهُمۡ وَرَضُو<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>اۡ</span> عَنۡهُ‌ۚ ذ<rule class=custom_alef_maksora>ٰ</rule>لِكَ لِمَنۡ خَشِىَ رَبَّهُۥ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>99:6</strong> — يَوۡمَئِذٍ يَصۡدُرُ ٱلنَّاسُ أَشۡتَاتًا لِّيُرَوۡ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>اۡ</span> أَعۡمَـٰلَهُمۡ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
<p><strong>103:3</strong> — إِلَّا ٱلَّذِينَ ءَامَنُو<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>اۡ</span> وَعَمِلُو<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>اۡ</span> ٱلصَّـٰلِحَـٰتِ وَتَوَاصَوۡ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>اۡ</span> بِٱلۡحَقِّ وَتَوَاصَوۡ<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>اۡ</span> بِٱلصَّبۡرِ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 4)</span></p>
<p><strong>106:3</strong> — فَلۡيَعۡبُدُو<span style='color:red;font-weight:bold'>اۡ</span> رَبَّ هَـٰذَا ٱلۡبَيۡتِ <span style='color:gray'>(Occurrences in verse: 1)</span></p>
